<div id="review_1407898713" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1407898713" />
    <a title="Robin (Bridge Four)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14105531-robin-bridge-four"><img alt="Robin (Bridge Four)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473392517p2/14105531.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1407898713?book_show_action=true">Oct 03, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Robin (Bridge Four)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Robin (Bridge Four)" href="/user/show/14105531-robin-bridge-four">Robin (Bridge Four)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=cotton-candy">cotton-candy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=chick-i-want-to-hang-out-with">chick-i-want-to-hang-out-with</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=chocolate-pms-day-reads">chocolate-pms-day-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=4-5-stars">4-5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=book-boyfriend-material">book-boyfriend-material</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=sexy">sexy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1407898713" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12043624057090243401"><b>4.5 Reformed Rake Stars</b><br/><br/>I was really ready not to like this book. I was totally loving St. Vincent in the last one until….well you know what he did.<br/><blockquote>
  <i>“He didn’t seem to take it well, my borrowing of his betrothed.”<br/>“You k-kidnapped her,” Evangeline countered calmly. “‘Borrowing’ implies that you intended to give her back.”</i>
</blockquote><br/>But it seems that our little stammering Evie is just as desperate if not even more so than St. Vincent and needs a husband quick. Evie has way more strength and gumption than I</span>
  <span id="freeText12043624057090243401" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Reformed Rake Stars</b><br /><br />I was really ready not to like this book. I was totally loving St. Vincent in the last one until….well you know what he did.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>“He didn’t seem to take it well, my borrowing of his betrothed.”<br />“You k-kidnapped her,” Evangeline countered calmly. “‘Borrowing’ implies that you intended to give her back.”</i>
</blockquote><br />But it seems that our little stammering Evie is just as desperate if not even more so than St. Vincent and needs a husband quick. Evie has way more strength and gumption than I had initially thought. Who knew that behind that little stammer and shy façade was someone so stubborn, determined and strong. I mean not just anyone can take on the dastardly rake St. Vincent is.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>“It’s not a love match. It’s a marriage of convenience, and there’s not enough warmth between us to light a birthday candle. Get on with it, if you please. Neither of us has had a proper sleep in two days.”<br />Silence fell over the scene, with MacPhee and his two daughters appearing shocked by the brusque remarks. Then the blacksmith’s heavy brows lowered over his eyes in a scowl. “I don’t like ye,” he announced.<br />St. Vincent regarded him with exasperation. “Neither does my bride-to-be. But since that’s not going to stop her from marrying me, it shouldn’t stop you either. Go on.”</i>
</blockquote><br />I’ll admit I couldn’t hold my grudge and distain for St Vincent. I grew to like him again quite soon as I’m thrown with Evie into their marriage of convenience. What is it with Jerky guys that are so broken you just want to fix them? Also it was quite obvious from very early that St. Vincent did care a lot for Evie, even though he never knew how to say the words he showed her with all of his deeds. But Evie oh our girl has been treated badly with words and deeds by her family for as long as she can remember and finally she feels comfortable and safe enough with someone to fight back with them.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>“At the moment you’re too much of a novice to be worth the bother,” he continued coolly. “Perhaps I’ll seduce you in the future, after some other men have taken the trouble to educate you.”<br />“I doubt it,” she said sullenly. “I would never be so bourgeois as to sleep with my own husband.”<br />A catch of laughter escaped him. “My God. You must have been waiting for days to use that one. Congratulations, child. We haven’t yet been married a week, and you’re already learning how to fight.”</i>
</blockquote><br />Evie was sure that after the marriage and initial consummation he would be ready to be rid of her. However, instead of just taking the money and moving on Evie’s challenges have made him want to rise to the occasion and turn her father’s club into something great again. He just has some growing to do and maybe with the help of Cam (who is totally adorable by the way) he might just learn a few things.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>“You fault me for having standards?” Sebastian countered icily. <br />“Not at all. I fault you for having two sets of them. The Rom have a saying—‘With one behind, you cannot sit on two horses.’</i>
</blockquote><br />I enjoyed the growth of Sebastian St. Vincent and I loved how Evie really came into her own away from her dreadful family. The danger felt pretty real and the way it brought the couple closer together was so much fun and what I really love in Historical Romances.<br /><br />Another fun read in the Wallflowers series.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="12043624057090243401" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1946620723" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1946620723" />
    <a title="Amy | Foxy Blogs" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs"><img alt="Amy | Foxy Blogs" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1366176904p2/9955253.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1946620723?book_show_action=true">Mar 19, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Amy | Foxy Blogs" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amy | Foxy Blogs" href="/user/show/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs">Amy | Foxy Blogs</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs?shelf=headphones">headphones</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs?shelf=library2go">library2go</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs?shelf=2017-books">2017-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs?shelf=march-2017">march-2017</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1946620723" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1736971566698205814"><br/><b>FOUR POINT FIVE STARS</b><br/><br/><b>THE HUSBAND HUNTERS ARE BACK!</b><br/>In London (1843) a pact is made between 4 wallflowers. They will help each other find husbands starting with the oldest and working down to the youngest. <br/><br/>(1) Annabelle is the oldest of the pact. Married - first book.<br/>(2) Lillian is a rich American who has not acclimated to England.<br/>(3) <b>Evie</b> is painfully shy and stutters.<br/>(4) Daisy is the younger sister to Lillian. <br/><br/><b>Evie</b> is in a predicament where her relatives are going to marry her off to her cousin </span>
  <span id="freeText1736971566698205814" style="display:none"><br><b>FOUR POINT FIVE STARS</b><br><br><b>THE HUSBAND HUNTERS ARE BACK!</b><br>In London (1843) a pact is made between 4 wallflowers. They will help each other find husbands starting with the oldest and working down to the youngest. <br><br>(1) Annabelle is the oldest of the pact. Married - first book.<br>(2) Lillian is a rich American who has not acclimated to England.<br>(3) <b>Evie</b> is painfully shy and stutters.<br>(4) Daisy is the younger sister to Lillian. <br><br><b>Evie</b> is in a predicament where her relatives are going to marry her off to her cousin so when her father dies his wealth will stay within the family. She’s not fond of her relatives because they are mean to her and have kept her from being with her dying father. <br><br>Impulsively, Evie asks the rake Viscount St. Vincent (<b>Sebastian</b>) to marry her to avoid being married to her cousin. To her delight, he agrees to this marriage of convenience. Because of the situation, Evie is not concerned about his faithfulness. But like any good rake on his way to being reformed he wants to prove he can be a one-woman-man. To have him prove himself Evie tells him no sex for 3 months after the wedding night. He's up for the challenge.<br><br>I really enjoyed listening to this audio. Evie’s growth from an intimidated young woman to a strong woman not afraid to speak her mind happened gradually over the course of the book. At the beginning of the book, you notice Evie stutters a lot but part way through you forget that she ever had that issue prior. <br><br>I was all ready to read <b>Devil in Spring</b> book 3 in <i>The Ravenels Series</i> when I found out the hero is the son of Evie &amp; Sebastian from this book. Even though it’s not necessary to first read this book before reading <u>Devil in Spring</u> I figured I would go ahead and read it. Ms. Kleypas writes her books so they can be read as standalones but if you want you can read them in order to see how other characters in series join into the stories. I’ve heard Cam from this book (Devil in Winter) is the hero in <u>Mine till Midnight.</u> I’m looking forward to reading about him after meeting him in this book. I only have one wallflower left to read about before I can move onto Cam’s book. <br><br>If you like historical romance then this series is a great one to read. <br><br><br><b>SERIES:</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/114162.Secrets_of_a_Summer_Night__Wallflowers___1_" title="Secrets of a Summer Night (Wallflowers, #1) by Lisa Kleypas" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1298443922s/114162.jpg" alt="Secrets of a Summer Night (Wallflowers, #1) by Lisa Kleypas" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/827412.It_Happened_One_Autumn__Wallflowers___2_" title="It Happened One Autumn (Wallflowers, #2) by Lisa Kleypas" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1388206425s/827412.jpg" alt="It Happened One Autumn (Wallflowers, #2) by Lisa Kleypas" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/114166.Devil_in_Winter__Wallflowers___3_" title="Devil in Winter (Wallflowers, #3) by Lisa Kleypas" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1309220205s/114166.jpg" alt="Devil in Winter (Wallflowers, #3) by Lisa Kleypas" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/105574.Scandal_in_Spring__Wallflowers___4_" title="Scandal in Spring (Wallflowers, #4) by Lisa Kleypas" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1452549904s/105574.jpg" alt="Scandal in Spring (Wallflowers, #4) by Lisa Kleypas" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/3050104.A_Wallflower_Christmas__Wallflowers___4_5_" title="A Wallflower Christmas (Wallflowers, #4.5) by Lisa Kleypas" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1442883779s/3050104.jpg" alt="A Wallflower Christmas (Wallflowers, #4.5) by Lisa Kleypas" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Can be read as standalones but it's recommended reading the series in order.<br><i>Prequel:</i><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/674220.Again_the_Magic__Wallflowers___0_5_" title="Again the Magic (Wallflowers, #0.5) by Lisa Kleypas" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1418771403s/674220.jpg" alt="Again the Magic (Wallflowers, #0.5) by Lisa Kleypas" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>(#0.5)<br>*****************************************<br><b>Wallflowers series is followed by The Hathaway series:</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/693016.Mine_Till_Midnight__The_Hathaways___1_" title="Mine Till Midnight (The Hathaways, #1) by Lisa Kleypas" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1380326170s/693016.jpg" alt="Mine Till Midnight (The Hathaways, #1) by Lisa Kleypas" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/2948832.Seduce_Me_at_Sunrise__The_Hathaways___2_" title="Seduce Me at Sunrise (The Hathaways, #2) by Lisa Kleypas" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1390526497s/2948832.jpg" alt="Seduce Me at Sunrise (The Hathaways, #2) by Lisa Kleypas" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_2967162642" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2967162642" />
    <a title="Sandra ~ ♥ Cross My Heart ♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17716247-sandra-cross-my-heart"><img alt="Sandra ~ ♥ Cross My Heart ♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1415483040p2/17716247.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2967162642?book_show_action=true">Sep 10, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sandra ~ ♥ Cross My Heart ♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sandra ~ ♥ Cross My Heart ♥" href="/user/show/17716247-sandra-cross-my-heart">Sandra ~ ♥ Cross My Heart ♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/6641611-devil-in-winter">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17716247-sandra-cross-my-heart?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17716247-sandra-cross-my-heart?shelf=romance-historical">romance-historical</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17716247-sandra-cross-my-heart?shelf=favorites-2019">favorites-2019</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2967162642" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6379401955254521798">If anyone had told me I'd one day pull for the scum ball Sebastian, Lord St. Vincent (actually some did!), after I finished reading <i>It Happened One Autumn</i>, I would have said <i>"you're crazy"</i>! However, I stand here today eating my words after reading <i>Devil In Winter</i>. Kleypas wove an amazing magic spell and transformed two misfits into an endearing couple, revealing a softer, more vulnerable side of both. Evie's on the run from her maternal relatives because they've threatened her with a forced marr</span>
  <span id="freeText6379401955254521798" style="display:none">If anyone had told me I'd one day pull for the scum ball Sebastian, Lord St. Vincent (actually some did!), after I finished reading <i>It Happened One Autumn</i>, I would have said <i>"you're crazy"</i>! However, I stand here today eating my words after reading <i>Devil In Winter</i>. Kleypas wove an amazing magic spell and transformed two misfits into an endearing couple, revealing a softer, more vulnerable side of both. Evie's on the run from her maternal relatives because they've threatened her with a forced marriage to her own cousin in an effort to gain control of her fortune. I found Evie to be shy and awkward. . . and yes, even <i>forgettable</i>, in previous books, as she struggled with an embarrassing stutter, but she displays a braver, more forward side in this book. Evie steps outside her comfort zone and calls on the infamous rogue Lord St. Vincent in his home with a brazen offer he can't refuse - marry and protect her and her fortune is his. Sebastian was an arrogant womanizer in previous books - a desperate man on the verge of losing everything. While he's shocked by Evie's offer, he quickly realizes it's the answer to all his problems and thus their odd joining begins. Watching Sebastian's interaction with Evie is a pure delight as his honesty and humor reveal a different man beneath the badboy facade. Evie knows she's made a deal with the devil. Will she live to regret it?<br /><br />Nobody does Historical Romance better than Lisa Kleypas! Nobody! Her writing is always picturesque, flowing flawlessly as she manipulates scenes and breathes life into characters with depth, personality, and believable qualities. The author's ability to take two characters who appear to be polar-opposites and bring them together in such a way that causes readers to pull for them is nothing short of amazing. They don't always fall in love willingly, but fall they will. The banter and sexual tension ramps up as the story unfolds as does the suspense and sense of urgency. Series readers will love the support cast including characters from previous books. <i>Devil In Winter</i> is a fantastic addition to the Wallflower series, and I highly recommend it to fans of historical romance.<br />4.5 Amazing Stars!<br />Reviewed at <a href="https://crossmyheartbookreviews.blogspot.com/2019/09/devil-in-winter-review.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Cross My Heart Reviews</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="6379401955254521798" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1755557200" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1755557200" />
    <a title="Nenia ✨️ Socially Awkward Trash Panda ✨️ Campbell" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2190064-nenia-socially-awkward-trash-panda-campbell"><img alt="Nenia ✨️ Socially Awkward Trash Panda ✨️ Campbell" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1584062476p2/2190064.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1755557200?book_show_action=true">Sep 11, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nenia ✨️ Socially Awkward Trash Panda ✨️ Campbell" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nenia ✨️ Socially Awkward Trash Panda ✨️ Campbell" href="/user/show/2190064-nenia-socially-awkward-trash-panda-campbell">Nenia ✨️ Socially Awkward Trash Panda ✨️ Campbell</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/6641611-devil-in-winter">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2190064-nenia-socially-awkward-trash-panda-campbell?shelf=kissing-books">kissing-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2190064-nenia-socially-awkward-trash-panda-campbell?shelf=victorian">victorian</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2190064-nenia-socially-awkward-trash-panda-campbell?shelf=historical-romance">historical-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1755557200" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17646298553658786314"><a href='http://readasaurus.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1459070464i/18565492.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><a href='https://www.instagram.com/neniagram/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Instagram</a> || <a href='https://twitter.com/NeniaCampbell' rel='nofollow noopener'>Twitter</a> || <a href='https://www.facebook.com/aficionenias/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Facebook</a> || <a href='http://www.amazon.com/Nenia-Campbell/e/B00AWVRKMS' rel='nofollow noopener'>Amazon</a> || <a href='https://www.pinterest.com/mightbeamisprin/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Pinterest</a><br/><br/><br/>I've heard about the "polarizing" event in the previous book that caused so many people to hate Sebastian, Lord St. Vincent. I also agree with what others are saying; that despite all the other characters in the book telling the readers, repeatedly, what a villain he is, he sure doesn't walk the walk (apart from that one incident). If I'm going to suck it up and read a book about a rake and a virgin, then by God, I want a man who is in <i>d</i></span>
  <span id="freeText17646298553658786314" style="display:none"><a href="http://readasaurus.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1459070464i/18565492.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="https://www.instagram.com/neniagram/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> || <a href="https://twitter.com/NeniaCampbell" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> || <a href="https://www.facebook.com/aficionenias/" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> || <a href="http://www.amazon.com/Nenia-Campbell/e/B00AWVRKMS" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon</a> || <a href="https://www.pinterest.com/mightbeamisprin/" rel="nofollow noopener">Pinterest</a><br><br><br>I've heard about the "polarizing" event in the previous book that caused so many people to hate Sebastian, Lord St. Vincent. I also agree with what others are saying; that despite all the other characters in the book telling the readers, repeatedly, what a villain he is, he sure doesn't walk the walk (apart from that one incident). If I'm going to suck it up and read a book about a rake and a virgin, then by God, I want a man who is in <i>desperate </i>need of reformation. That's one of the reasons <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1601088306" rel="nofollow noopener">I liked Elizabeth Hoyt's DUKE OF SIN so much</a>. Valentine Napier played every single jerk card in his hand.<br><br><br><br>Our story kicks off with Evangeline Jenner demanding an audience with notorious rake, St. Vincent. She has an offer he can't refuse. Her father is on his deathbed, and plans to leave her all the money from his gaming den, Jenner's. Knowing this, her greedy relations have been keeping her prisoner, starving and beating her, and refusing to let her visit him. Their plan is to force her to marry her cousin so that her inheritance will be in his control, and <i>then</i>, Evie suspects that their plan is to arrange her death in some way so that they can spend the money freely.<br><br><br><br>The only way to escape this fate is by elopement. She proposes a marriage of convenience. In exchange for her money, St. Vincent will grant her freedom - freedom from her relatives, freedom to visit her father, freedom to live with the protection of his title. Obviously - it's not a love match.<br><br><br><br>Lisa Kleypas can be hit or miss with me. I like her writing style a lot - it's very clean and spare, she really has a sense for how much description to give and how to balance dialogue and narrative. The problems are her characters. Sometimes her "strong" heroines are just plain bitchy, and sometimes her "sweet" heroines are just spineless doormats that people use for sh*t-sticking practice. Also, her alpha heroes are sometimes just Grade-A jerks who make me hate them. Irredeemably so.<br><br><br><br>Evie was an okay heroine. Nothing too special. She's a stammering virgin - literally - who ends up redeeming a rake with her meekness and her humility and her innocence. *cue eye roll here* Been there, done that, gotten the t-shirt, honey. What else you got? She has a couple more vertebrae than other heroines cast in her mold, and I did like that she at least tried to stick up for herself and for the most part, spoke her mind when it counted. Evie won't be topping any of my favorites lists by any means, but she isn't on my sh*t list, either. Let's just say that she's...inoffensive.<br><br><br><br>My feelings about St. Vincent are a little more complicated. I don't really like that he's hanging out in alpha limbo. He's a bit too...courtly to be straight up gamma/alpha, but he's way too rapey and chauvinistic for me to accept him as a "nice" hero. His constant bragging about his prowess definitely garnered an eye-roll or two from me. That said, he had some great lines. Sexy lines. He's the perfect example of a character who you might find sexually attractive but would make a sh*tty boyfriend.<br><br><br><br>On that note, the romance is pretty slow-burn, although the sex happens early on in the story (instead of that magical 3/4s point that so many books insist on adhering to). Towards the end, I found it hilarious, the lengths that St. Vincent would go to deny his attraction to Evie. They bickered too much, though, and when their arguments started getting redundant, I began to eye the page count.<br><br><br><br>Also, what's with Kleypas and her fondness for attempted murder subplots? &gt;_&gt;<br><br><br><br>DEVIL IN WINTER is a decent romance. It kind of reminded me of <i>The Gamblers </i>duology (which is appropriate in more ways than one, because she makes reference to Craven's in here, which made me happy). In particular, DEVIL reminded me of DREAMING OF YOU, because St. Vincent is like a "well-bred" version of Derek Craven - and both of them are just as stubborn as mules when it comes to dragging their heels about admitting their feelings. Nothing will surpass the love I feel for THEN CAME YOU, though: Alex, Lord Wolverton is the OG of Lisa Kleypas love interests. #SorryNotSorry<br><br><br><br>3.5 stars.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17646298553658786314" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

It was the simplest of all the rings, a polished gold band engraved with the words Tha Gad Agam Ort. “What does this mean?” she asked MacPhee. “It says, ‘My love is upon ye.’”</blockquote>

He did reform rather quickly though after his debacle in the previous book. And then, there was no going back. <br><b>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('SBIPgGbHfupk3nOeXgBUGQQjpAk6bbqQ6ObAEDFdcEPJzj+rOQTWrqOD4JwDx6rj25yVmdpDqlxf2GVyaTeKEQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('cHWxWznC/OmaOKKOuPO65MWWlonBN/X2uumgoG33a0PxqYFwZgFUrV1lMYzlNEQeGimnGSEZ5ToN1wXCNZ2REQ==')})
  }
